# Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Streams DSL (map, filter, groupBy) and their corresponding Processor API equivalents, to support a team migrating from DSL to lower-level Processor API for custom state store management.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Analysis\\n\\nThe Apache Kafka Streams framework provides two complementary layers for stream processing: the high-level Kafka Streams DSL (Domain Specific Language) in the kstream package and the lower-level Processor API for advanced use cases requiring custom state store management.\\n\\n### DSL Layer (High-Level Abstraction)\\nThe DSL is defined through three main interfaces in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/`:\\n- **KStream.java**: The primary stateless stream abstraction with operations: filter(), filterNot(), map(), mapValues(), flatMap(), flatMapValues(), branch(), groupBy(), groupByKey(), aggregate(), reduce(), foreach(), peek(), print(), process(), processValues(), transform(), and transformValues()\\n- **KGroupedStream.java**: Result of groupBy() operation, providing: aggregate(), reduce(), count()\\n- **KTable.java**: Stateful table abstraction with: filter(), filterNot(), mapValues(), transformValues(), toStream()\\n- **KGroupedTable.java**: Result of groupBy() on KTable\\n- **GlobalKTable.java**: Broadcast table for joins\\n\\nAdditional transformer interfaces for stateful operations:\\n- Transformer.java, TransformerSupplier.java: For custom stateful transformations\\n- ValueTransformer.java, ValueTransformerWithKey.java: For value-only transformations with state\\n\\n### DSL Implementation Classes\\nThe actual implementations are in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/`:\\n- **KStreamImpl.java**: Implements the KStream interface with method delegation\\n- **KGroupedStreamImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedStream with GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder\\n- **KTableImpl.java**: Implements KTable interface\\n- **KGroupedTableImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedTable interface\\n- **GlobalKTableImpl.java**: Implements GlobalKTable interface\\n\\n### Processor API Implementation Layer\\nThe core stateless and stateful operations are implemented as ProcessorSupplier classes that create Processor instances:\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using FixedKeyProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamFilter.java**: Implements filter(Predicate) via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n- **KStreamMapValues.java**: Implements mapValues() via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier\\n- **KStreamPeek.java**: Implements peek() for side effects\\n- **ForeachProcessor.java**: Implements foreach() action\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using ProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamMap.java**: Implements map() via ProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n- **KStreamFlatMap.java**: Implements flatMap()\\n- **KStreamFlatMapValues.java**: Implements flatMapValues()\\n- **KStreamBranch.java**: Implements branch() conditional routing\\n- **KStreamPrint.java**: Implements print() debug output\\n\\n#### Stateful Processors (Aggregation and Windowing):\\n- **KStreamAggregate.java**: Implements aggregate() after groupBy for streaming aggregation\\n- **KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java**: ProcessorSupplier for stream aggregation\\n- **KStreamReduce.java**: Implements reduce() operation\\n- **KStreamWindowAggregate.java**: Time-windowed aggregation processor\\n- **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java**: Session-windowed aggregation\\n- **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java**: Sliding window aggregation\\n\\n#### Table Processors:\\n- **KTableFilter.java**: Filter operation on KTable\\n- **KTableMapValues.java**: Transform values on KTable\\n- **KTableAggregate.java**: Aggregation on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableReduce.java**: Reduce on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableTransformValues.java**: Stateful value transformation on KTable\\n- **KTablePassThrough.java**: Identity transformation\\n- **KTableSource.java**: Source for KTable from topics\\n- **KTableRepartitionMap.java**: Repartitioning for groupBy\\n- **KTableProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for KTable processors\\n\\n#### Join Processors:\\n- **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java**: Stream-GlobalTable join processor\\n- **KStreamKStreamJoin.java**: Stream-Stream join processor\\n- **KStreamKTableJoin.java**: Stream-Table join processor\\n- **KTableKTableJoinMerger.java**: Table-Table join merger\\n\\n### Core Processor API Interfaces\\nThe foundation for all custom processor implementations in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/`:\\n- **Processor.java**: Base interface for processors that can transform both key and value\\n- **ProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory interface creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor.java**: Optimized processor for fixed-key operations (key unchanged)\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n- **ContextualProcessor.java**: Base class providing context access for stateful operations\\n- **ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java**: Base class for fixed-key stateful processors\\n- **ProcessorContext.java**: Interface for accessing topology context, state stores, and forwarding records\\n- **Record.java**: Container for key-value-timestamp-headers data\\n\\nLegacy interfaces:\\n- **ProcessorContext.java** (org.apache.kafka.streams.processor): Legacy processor context\\n- **StateStore.java**: Interface for managed state storage\\n\\n### Migration Path from DSL to Processor API\\n\\n**Step 1: Replace DSL chains with custom processors**\\n```\\n// DSL\\nKStream<String, String> stream = builder.stream(\\\"input\\\");\\nstream.filter((k, v) -> v.startsWith(\\\"error\\\"))\\n      .map((k, v) -> new KeyValue<>(k, v.toUpperCase()))\\n      .to(\\\"output\\\");\\n\\n// Processor API\\nTopology topology = new Topology();\\ntopology.addSource(\\\"source\\\", \\\"input\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"filter\\\", () -> new MyFilterProcessor(), \\\"source\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"map\\\", () -> new MyMapProcessor(), \\\"filter\\\")\\n        .addSink(\\\"sink\\\", \\\"output\\\", \\\"map\\\");\\n```\\n\\n**Step 2: Implement custom processors**\\nExtend `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor` (for fixed-key operations) or `ContextualProcessor` (for key/value transformations):\\n- Override `process(Record<K, V> record)` method\\n- Access context via `context()` method\\n- Forward records using `context().forward(record)`\\n- Access state stores via `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\n**Step 3: Manage custom state stores**\\nFor operations requiring state (aggregation, joins, windowing):\\n- Define state store suppliers\\n- Attach to processors via `topology.addStateStore(storeBuilder, processorNames...)`\\n- Access in custom processor via ProcessorContext.getStateStore()\\n\\n**Key Benefits of Processor API Migration:**\\n- Fine-grained control over state store management\\n- Custom state store implementations for specialized use cases\\n- Direct access to record metadata (timestamps, headers, offsets)\\n- Optimized performance for specific workloads\\n- Custom caching and eviction policies\\n\\n### Files in apache/kafka Repository\\nAll files are located under `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/`, with the primary migration path requiring understanding of:\\n- `kstream/KStream.java` (DSL interface)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java` (DSL implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java` (example: filter processor implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java` (example: map processor implementation)\\n- `processor/api/Processor.java` (base Processor API)\\n- `processor/api/ProcessorContext.java` (context for state store access)\"\n}\n",

Analysis\\n\\nThe Apache Kafka Streams framework provides two complementary layers for stream processing: the high-level Kafka Streams DSL (Domain Specific Language) in the kstream package and the lower-level Processor API for advanced use cases requiring custom state store management.\\n\\n### DSL Layer (High-Level Abstraction)\\nThe DSL is defined through three main interfaces in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/`:\\n- **KStream.java**: The primary stateless stream abstraction with operations: filter(), filterNot(), map(), mapValues(), flatMap(), flatMapValues(), branch(), groupBy(), groupByKey(), aggregate(), reduce(), foreach(), peek(), print(), process(), processValues(), transform(), and transformValues()\\n- **KGroupedStream.java**: Result of groupBy() operation, providing: aggregate(), reduce(), count()\\n- **KTable.java**: Stateful table abstraction with: filter(), filterNot(), mapValues(), transformValues(), toStream()\\n- **KGroupedTable.java**: Result of groupBy() on KTable\\n- **GlobalKTable.java**: Broadcast table for joins\\n\\nAdditional transformer interfaces for stateful operations:\\n- Transformer.java, TransformerSupplier.java: For custom stateful transformations\\n- ValueTransformer.java, ValueTransformerWithKey.java: For value-only transformations with state\\n\\n### DSL Implementation Classes\\nThe actual implementations are in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/`:\\n- **KStreamImpl.java**: Implements the KStream interface with method delegation\\n- **KGroupedStreamImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedStream with GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder\\n- **KTableImpl.java**: Implements KTable interface\\n- **KGroupedTableImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedTable interface\\n- **GlobalKTableImpl.java**: Implements GlobalKTable interface\\n\\n### Processor API Implementation Layer\\nThe core stateless and stateful operations are implemented as ProcessorSupplier classes that create Processor instances:\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using FixedKeyProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamFilter.java**: Implements filter(Predicate) via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n- **KStreamMapValues.java**: Implements mapValues() via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier\\n- **KStreamPeek.java**: Implements peek() for side effects\\n- **ForeachProcessor.java**: Implements foreach() action\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using ProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamMap.java**: Implements map() via ProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n- **KStreamFlatMap.java**: Implements flatMap()\\n- **KStreamFlatMapValues.java**: Implements flatMapValues()\\n- **KStreamBranch.java**: Implements branch() conditional routing\\n- **KStreamPrint.java**: Implements print() debug output\\n\\n#### Stateful Processors (Aggregation and Windowing):\\n- **KStreamAggregate.java**: Implements aggregate() after groupBy for streaming aggregation\\n- **KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java**: ProcessorSupplier for stream aggregation\\n- **KStreamReduce.java**: Implements reduce() operation\\n- **KStreamWindowAggregate.java**: Time-windowed aggregation processor\\n- **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java**: Session-windowed aggregation\\n- **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java**: Sliding window aggregation\\n\\n#### Table Processors:\\n- **KTableFilter.java**: Filter operation on KTable\\n- **KTableMapValues.java**: Transform values on KTable\\n- **KTableAggregate.java**: Aggregation on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableReduce.java**: Reduce on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableTransformValues.java**: Stateful value transformation on KTable\\n- **KTablePassThrough.java**: Identity transformation\\n- **KTableSource.java**: Source for KTable from topics\\n- **KTableRepartitionMap.java**: Repartitioning for groupBy\\n- **KTableProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for KTable processors\\n\\n#### Join Processors:\\n- **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java**: Stream-GlobalTable join processor\\n- **KStreamKStreamJoin.java**: Stream-Stream join processor\\n- **KStreamKTableJoin.java**: Stream-Table join processor\\n- **KTableKTableJoinMerger.java**: Table-Table join merger\\n\\n### Core Processor API Interfaces\\nThe foundation for all custom processor implementations in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/`:\\n- **Processor.java**: Base interface for processors that can transform both key and value\\n- **ProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory interface creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor.java**: Optimized processor for fixed-key operations (key unchanged)\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n- **ContextualProcessor.java**: Base class providing context access for stateful operations\\n- **ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java**: Base class for fixed-key stateful processors\\n- **ProcessorContext.java**: Interface for accessing topology context, state stores, and forwarding records\\n- **Record.java**: Container for key-value-timestamp-headers data\\n\\nLegacy interfaces:\\n- **ProcessorContext.java** (org.apache.kafka.streams.processor): Legacy processor context\\n- **StateStore.java**: Interface for managed state storage\\n\\n### Migration Path from DSL to Processor API\\n\\n**Step 1: Replace DSL chains with custom processors**\\n```\\n// DSL\\nKStream<String, String> stream = builder.stream(\\\"input\\\");\\nstream.filter((k, v) -> v.startsWith(\\\"error\\\"))\\n      .map((k, v) -> new KeyValue<>(k, v.toUpperCase()))\\n      .to(\\\"output\\\");\\n\\n// Processor API\\nTopology topology = new Topology();\\ntopology.addSource(\\\"source\\\", \\\"input\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"filter\\\", () -> new MyFilterProcessor(), \\\"source\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"map\\\", () -> new MyMapProcessor(), \\\"filter\\\")\\n        .addSink(\\\"sink\\\", \\\"output\\\", \\\"map\\\");\\n```\\n\\n**Step 2: Implement custom processors**\\nExtend `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor` (for fixed-key operations) or `ContextualProcessor` (for key/value transformations):\\n- Override `process(Record<K, V> record)` method\\n- Access context via `context()` method\\n- Forward records using `context().forward(record)`\\n- Access state stores via `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\n**Step 3: Manage custom state stores**\\nFor operations requiring state (aggregation, joins, windowing):\\n- Define state store suppliers\\n- Attach to processors via `topology.addStateStore(storeBuilder, processorNames...)`\\n- Access in custom processor via ProcessorContext.getStateStore()\\n\\n**Key Benefits of Processor API Migration:**\\n- Fine-grained control over state store management\\n- Custom state store implementations for specialized use cases\\n- Direct access to record metadata (timestamps, headers, offsets)\\n- Optimized performance for specific workloads\\n- Custom caching and eviction policies\\n\\n### Files in apache/kafka Repository\\nAll files are located under `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/`, with the primary migration path requiring understanding of:\\n- `kstream/KStream.java` (DSL interface)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java` (DSL implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java` (example: filter processor implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java` (example: map processor implementation)\\n- `processor/api/Processor.java` (base Processor API)\\n- `processor/api/ProcessorContext.java` (context for state store access)\"\n}\n",

provides high-level abstractions for stream processing that are implemented via the lower-level Processor API. Key findings:\\n\\n**DSL Layer (kstream package):**\\n- KStream.java contains the primary DSL interface with methods like filter(), map(), mapValues(), flatMap(), flatMapValues(), groupBy(), groupByKey(), aggregate(), reduce(), foreach(), and peek().\\n- KGroupedStream.java represents the result of groupBy() operations and provides aggregation methods (aggregate, reduce, count).\\n- KTable.java provides table operations including filter(), filterNot(), and mapValues().\\n- These interfaces are implemented by KStreamImpl, KGroupedStreamImpl, and KTableImpl classes in the internals directory.\\n\\n**Processor API Layer (processor/api and kstream/internals):**\\n- Core Processor API interfaces: Processor, ProcessorSupplier, FixedKeyProcessor, FixedKeyProcessorSupplier, ContextualProcessor, ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.\\n- DSL operations are implemented as ProcessorSupplier implementations:\\n  * KStreamFilter implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier for filter operations\\n  * KStreamMap implements ProcessorSupplier for map operations (changes both key and value)\\n  * KStreamMapValues implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier for mapValues operations (preserves key)\\n  * KStreamFlatMap and KStreamFlatMapValues for flat mapping operations\\n  * KStreamAggregate and KStreamReduce for stateful aggregation after groupBy\\n  * KTableFilter, KTableMapValues, KTableAggregate, KTableReduce for table operations\\n  * ForeachProcessor for foreach actions, KStreamPeek for peek operations, KStreamPrint for print\\n\\n**Migration Path:**\\nTeams migrating from DSL to Processor API should:\\n1. Replace KStream DSL operations with custom Processor/FixedKeyProcessor implementations\\n2. Implement ProcessorSupplier or FixedKeyProcessorSupplier instead of DSL method chains\\n3. Use Topology.addProcessor() to wire custom processors for state store management\\n4. Access state stores via ProcessorContext.getStateStore() for custom state management\\n\\n**Files in apache/kafka repository:**\\n- streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/KStream.java: DSL interface\\n- streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java: KStream implementation\\n- streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java: filter implementation\\n- streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java: map implementation\\n- streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java: Core Processor API\\n- streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/ProcessorContext.java: Legacy processor context for state store access\"\n}\n",

        "+  \"text\": \"## Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration - Complete Analysis\\n\\nThe Apache Kafka Streams framework provides two complementary layers for stream processing: the high-level Kafka Streams DSL (Domain Specific Language) in the kstream package and the lower-level Processor API for advanced use cases requiring custom state store management.\\n\\n### DSL Layer (High-Level Abstraction)\\nThe DSL is defined through three main interfaces in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/`:\\n- **KStream.java**: The primary stateless stream abstraction with operations: filter(), filterNot(), map(), mapValues(), flatMap(), flatMapValues(), branch(), groupBy(), groupByKey(), aggregate(), reduce(), foreach(), peek(), print(), process(), processValues(), transform(), and transformValues()\\n- **KGroupedStream.java**: Result of groupBy() operation, providing: aggregate(), reduce(), count()\\n- **KTable.java**: Stateful table abstraction with: filter(), filterNot(), mapValues(), transformValues(), toStream()\\n- **KGroupedTable.java**: Result of groupBy() on KTable\\n- **GlobalKTable.java**: Broadcast table for joins\\n\\nAdditional transformer interfaces for stateful operations:\\n- Transformer.java, TransformerSupplier.java: For custom stateful transformations\\n- ValueTransformer.java, ValueTransformerWithKey.java: For value-only transformations with state\\n\\n### DSL Implementation Classes\\nThe actual implementations are in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/`:\\n- **KStreamImpl.java**: Implements the KStream interface with method delegation\\n- **KGroupedStreamImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedStream with GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder\\n- **KTableImpl.java**: Implements KTable interface\\n- **KGroupedTableImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedTable interface\\n- **GlobalKTableImpl.java**: Implements GlobalKTable interface\\n\\n### Processor API Implementation Layer\\nThe core stateless and stateful operations are implemented as ProcessorSupplier classes that create Processor instances:\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using FixedKeyProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamFilter.java**: Implements filter(Predicate) via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n- **KStreamMapValues.java**: Implements mapValues() via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier\\n- **KStreamPeek.java**: Implements peek() for side effects\\n- **ForeachProcessor.java**: Implements foreach() action\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using ProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamMap.java**: Implements map() via ProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n- **KStreamFlatMap.java**: Implements flatMap()\\n- **KStreamFlatMapValues.java**: Implements flatMapValues()\\n- **KStreamBranch.java**: Implements branch() conditional routing\\n- **KStreamPrint.java**: Implements print() debug output\\n\\n#### Stateful Processors (Aggregation and Windowing):\\n- **KStreamAggregate.java**: Implements aggregate() after groupBy for streaming aggregation\\n- **KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java**: ProcessorSupplier for stream aggregation\\n- **KStreamReduce.java**: Implements reduce() operation\\n- **KStreamWindowAggregate.java**: Time-windowed aggregation processor\\n- **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java**: Session-windowed aggregation\\n- **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java**: Sliding window aggregation\\n\\n#### Table Processors:\\n- **KTableFilter.java**: Filter operation on KTable\\n- **KTableMapValues.java**: Transform values on KTable\\n- **KTableAggregate.java**: Aggregation on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableReduce.java**: Reduce on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableTransformValues.java**: Stateful value transformation on KTable\\n- **KTablePassThrough.java**: Identity transformation\\n- **KTableSource.java**: Source for KTable from topics\\n- **KTableRepartitionMap.java**: Repartitioning for groupBy\\n- **KTableProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for KTable processors\\n\\n#### Join Processors:\\n- **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java**: Stream-GlobalTable join processor\\n- **KStreamKStreamJoin.java**: Stream-Stream join processor\\n- **KStreamKTableJoin.java**: Stream-Table join processor\\n- **KTableKTableJoinMerger.java**: Table-Table join merger\\n\\n### Core Processor API Interfaces\\nThe foundation for all custom processor implementations in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/`:\\n- **Processor.java**: Base interface for processors that can transform both key and value\\n- **ProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory interface creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor.java**: Optimized processor for fixed-key operations (key unchanged)\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n- **ContextualProcessor.java**: Base class providing context access for stateful operations\\n- **ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java**: Base class for fixed-key stateful processors\\n- **ProcessorContext.java**: Interface for accessing topology context, state stores, and forwarding records\\n- **Record.java**: Container for key-value-timestamp-headers data\\n\\nLegacy interfaces:\\n- **ProcessorContext.java** (org.apache.kafka.streams.processor): Legacy processor context\\n- **StateStore.java**: Interface for managed state storage\\n\\n### Migration Path from DSL to Processor API\\n\\n**Step 1: Replace DSL chains with custom processors**\\n```\\n// DSL\\nKStream<String, String> stream = builder.stream(\\\"input\\\");\\nstream.filter((k, v) -> v.startsWith(\\\"error\\\"))\\n      .map((k, v) -> new KeyValue<>(k, v.toUpperCase()))\\n      .to(\\\"output\\\");\\n\\n// Processor API\\nTopology topology = new Topology();\\ntopology.addSource(\\\"source\\\", \\\"input\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"filter\\\", () -> new MyFilterProcessor(), \\\"source\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"map\\\", () -> new MyMapProcessor(), \\\"filter\\\")\\n        .addSink(\\\"sink\\\", \\\"output\\\", \\\"map\\\");\\n```\\n\\n**Step 2: Implement custom processors**\\nExtend `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor` (for fixed-key operations) or `ContextualProcessor` (for key/value transformations):\\n- Override `process(Record<K, V> record)` method\\n- Access context via `context()` method\\n- Forward records using `context().forward(record)`\\n- Access state stores via `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\n**Step 3: Manage custom state stores**\\nFor operations requiring state (aggregation, joins, windowing):\\n- Define state store suppliers\\n- Attach to processors via `topology.addStateStore(storeBuilder, processorNames...)`\\n- Access in custom processor via ProcessorContext.getStateStore()\\n\\n**Key Benefits of Processor API Migration:**\\n- Fine-grained control over state store management\\n- Custom state store implementations for specialized use cases\\n- Direct access to record metadata (timestamps, headers, offsets)\\n- Optimized performance for specific workloads\\n- Custom caching and eviction policies\\n\\n### Files in apache/kafka Repository\\nAll files are located under `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/`, with the primary migration path requiring understanding of:\\n- `kstream/KStream.java` (DSL interface)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java` (DSL implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java` (example: filter processor implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java` (example: map processor implementation)\\n- `processor/api/Processor.java` (base Processor API)\\n- `processor/api/ProcessorContext.java` (context for state store access)\"",

Analysis\\n\\nThe Apache Kafka Streams framework provides two complementary layers for stream processing: the high-level Kafka Streams DSL (Domain Specific Language) in the kstream package and the lower-level Processor API for advanced use cases requiring custom state store management.\\n\\n### DSL Layer (High-Level Abstraction)\\nThe DSL is defined through three main interfaces in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/`:\\n- **KStream.java**: The primary stateless stream abstraction with operations: filter(), filterNot(), map(), mapValues(), flatMap(), flatMapValues(), branch(), groupBy(), groupByKey(), aggregate(), reduce(), foreach(), peek(), print(), process(), processValues(), transform(), and transformValues()\\n- **KGroupedStream.java**: Result of groupBy() operation, providing: aggregate(), reduce(), count()\\n- **KTable.java**: Stateful table abstraction with: filter(), filterNot(), mapValues(), transformValues(), toStream()\\n- **KGroupedTable.java**: Result of groupBy() on KTable\\n- **GlobalKTable.java**: Broadcast table for joins\\n\\nAdditional transformer interfaces for stateful operations:\\n- Transformer.java, TransformerSupplier.java: For custom stateful transformations\\n- ValueTransformer.java, ValueTransformerWithKey.java: For value-only transformations with state\\n\\n### DSL Implementation Classes\\nThe actual implementations are in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/`:\\n- **KStreamImpl.java**: Implements the KStream interface with method delegation\\n- **KGroupedStreamImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedStream with GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder\\n- **KTableImpl.java**: Implements KTable interface\\n- **KGroupedTableImpl.java**: Implements KGroupedTable interface\\n- **GlobalKTableImpl.java**: Implements GlobalKTable interface\\n\\n### Processor API Implementation Layer\\nThe core stateless and stateful operations are implemented as ProcessorSupplier classes that create Processor instances:\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using FixedKeyProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamFilter.java**: Implements filter(Predicate) via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n- **KStreamMapValues.java**: Implements mapValues() via FixedKeyProcessorSupplier\\n- **KStreamPeek.java**: Implements peek() for side effects\\n- **ForeachProcessor.java**: Implements foreach() action\\n\\n#### Stateless Processors (using ProcessorSupplier):\\n- **KStreamMap.java**: Implements map() via ProcessorSupplier \u2192 KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n- **KStreamFlatMap.java**: Implements flatMap()\\n- **KStreamFlatMapValues.java**: Implements flatMapValues()\\n- **KStreamBranch.java**: Implements branch() conditional routing\\n- **KStreamPrint.java**: Implements print() debug output\\n\\n#### Stateful Processors (Aggregation and Windowing):\\n- **KStreamAggregate.java**: Implements aggregate() after groupBy for streaming aggregation\\n- **KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java**: ProcessorSupplier for stream aggregation\\n- **KStreamReduce.java**: Implements reduce() operation\\n- **KStreamWindowAggregate.java**: Time-windowed aggregation processor\\n- **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java**: Session-windowed aggregation\\n- **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java**: Sliding window aggregation\\n\\n#### Table Processors:\\n- **KTableFilter.java**: Filter operation on KTable\\n- **KTableMapValues.java**: Transform values on KTable\\n- **KTableAggregate.java**: Aggregation on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableReduce.java**: Reduce on grouped KTable\\n- **KTableTransformValues.java**: Stateful value transformation on KTable\\n- **KTablePassThrough.java**: Identity transformation\\n- **KTableSource.java**: Source for KTable from topics\\n- **KTableRepartitionMap.java**: Repartitioning for groupBy\\n- **KTableProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for KTable processors\\n\\n#### Join Processors:\\n- **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java**: Stream-GlobalTable join processor\\n- **KStreamKStreamJoin.java**: Stream-Stream join processor\\n- **KStreamKTableJoin.java**: Stream-Table join processor\\n- **KTableKTableJoinMerger.java**: Table-Table join merger\\n\\n### Core Processor API Interfaces\\nThe foundation for all custom processor implementations in `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/`:\\n- **Processor.java**: Base interface for processors that can transform both key and value\\n- **ProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory interface creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor.java**: Optimized processor for fixed-key operations (key unchanged)\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java**: Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n- **ContextualProcessor.java**: Base class providing context access for stateful operations\\n- **ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java**: Base class for fixed-key stateful processors\\n- **ProcessorContext.java**: Interface for accessing topology context, state stores, and forwarding records\\n- **Record.java**: Container for key-value-timestamp-headers data\\n\\nLegacy interfaces:\\n- **ProcessorContext.java** (org.apache.kafka.streams.processor): Legacy processor context\\n- **StateStore.java**: Interface for managed state storage\\n\\n### Migration Path from DSL to Processor API\\n\\n**Step 1: Replace DSL chains with custom processors**\\n```\\n// DSL\\nKStream<String, String> stream = builder.stream(\\\"input\\\");\\nstream.filter((k, v) -> v.startsWith(\\\"error\\\"))\\n      .map((k, v) -> new KeyValue<>(k, v.toUpperCase()))\\n      .to(\\\"output\\\");\\n\\n// Processor API\\nTopology topology = new Topology();\\ntopology.addSource(\\\"source\\\", \\\"input\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"filter\\\", () -> new MyFilterProcessor(), \\\"source\\\")\\n        .addProcessor(\\\"map\\\", () -> new MyMapProcessor(), \\\"filter\\\")\\n        .addSink(\\\"sink\\\", \\\"output\\\", \\\"map\\\");\\n```\\n\\n**Step 2: Implement custom processors**\\nExtend `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor` (for fixed-key operations) or `ContextualProcessor` (for key/value transformations):\\n- Override `process(Record<K, V> record)` method\\n- Access context via `context()` method\\n- Forward records using `context().forward(record)`\\n- Access state stores via `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\n**Step 3: Manage custom state stores**\\nFor operations requiring state (aggregation, joins, windowing):\\n- Define state store suppliers\\n- Attach to processors via `topology.addStateStore(storeBuilder, processorNames...)`\\n- Access in custom processor via ProcessorContext.getStateStore()\\n\\n**Key Benefits of Processor API Migration:**\\n- Fine-grained control over state store management\\n- Custom state store implementations for specialized use cases\\n- Direct access to record metadata (timestamps, headers, offsets)\\n- Optimized performance for specific workloads\\n- Custom caching and eviction policies\\n\\n### Files in apache/kafka Repository\\nAll files are located under `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/`, with the primary migration path requiring understanding of:\\n- `kstream/KStream.java` (DSL interface)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java` (DSL implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java` (example: filter processor implementation)\\n- `kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java` (example: map processor implementation)\\n- `processor/api/Processor.java` (base Processor API)\\n- `processor/api/ProcessorContext.java` (context for state store access)\"\n}"
